[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen processing XML entity declarations, specifically during parameter entity [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpansion. AddressSanitizer reports a READ of [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes at an address located [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately after a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte allocated heap region, resulting in an out-of-bounds [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **heap-buffer-overflow** vulnerability, specifically a multi-byte read [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation that attempts to access memory beyond the boundaries of an allocated heap[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during XML document parsing when the fuzzer processes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity declarations. The overflow occurs when `__asan_memcpy` is called from [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`, attempting to read [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes starting at address [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x502000000b37[0m[39m`. However, this address is located [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte region [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated at `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x502000000b30[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x502000000b37[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, meaning the read operation extends[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m bytes beyond the allocated buffer.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseInternalSubset`[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Entity processing**: `xmlParseEntityDecl` → `xmlParseEntityValue`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Parameter entity expansion**: `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Buffer operation**: `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` where the overflow occurs during [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memcpy`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Memory Allocation Context[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerable [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte buffer was originally allocated through:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `malloc` called by `xmlFuzzMalloc`[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `xmlStrndup` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `xmlStrdup` for string duplication[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `xmlCreateEntity` for entity creation[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `xmlAddEntity` to add the entity to the parser[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `xmlSAX2EntityDecl` as part of SAX2 entity declaration handling[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Size mismatch**: The code attempts to copy [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes into or from a buffer that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis only [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes long, indicating a significant miscalculation in buffer size [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequirements or bounds checking[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Entity value expansion**: The overflow occurs during parameter entity [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpansion [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, suggesting the vulnerability is triggered [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen processing entity references within entity values[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory safety issue**: The shadow bytes analysis shows the memory layout with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproper heap metadata [0m[1;39m([0m[39mredzone markers [0m[32m'fa'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, confirming the overflow detection is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccurate[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo understand the full scope of this vulnerability, the following code sections [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be examined:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **`[0m[35m/src/libxml2/[0m[95mparser.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m777[0m[39m`**: The `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` function, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparticularly the buffer size calculations and memcpy operation[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **`[0m[35m/src/libxml2/[0m[95mparser.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m4005[0m[39m`**: The `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` function to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand how parameter entities are expanded and how buffer sizes are determined[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **`[0m[35m/src/libxml2/[0m[95mparser.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m4119[0m[39m`**: The `xmlParseEntityValue` function for entity [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue parsing logic[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **`[0m[35m/src/libxml2/[0m[95mparser.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m5940[0m[39m`**: The `xmlParseEntityDecl` function for entity [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclaration handling[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **`[0m[35m/src/libxml2/[0m[95mentities.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m137[0m[39m`**: The `xmlCreateEntity` function to verify [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproper memory allocation for entity strings[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **`[0m[35m/src/libxml2/[0m[95mxmlstring.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m57[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m82[0m[39m`**: The `xmlStrndup` and `xmlStrdup` functions[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto ensure correct string duplication and size calculation[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe investigation should focus on understanding how buffer sizes are calculated [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring entity expansion, whether proper bounds checking is performed before memory [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations, and how the interaction between entity declaration parsing and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameter entity expansion could lead to this size discrepancy.[0m                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Problematic Code**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause**: Mismatched buffer and length parameters[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `ent->name`: Entity name string [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes for [0m[32m"myEntity"[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `ent->length`: Length of entity content/value [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, NOT the name [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code attempts to copy `ent->length` bytes from `ent->name`, causing a read of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m bytes from a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Evidence from Code Analysis[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entity Structure** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentities.[0m[1;92mc:153[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m154[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The `length` field explicitly stores [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, confirming it represents the content length, not the name [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Correct Pattern** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:4646[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The codebase demonstrates the proper way to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madd entity names:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddString[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&buf, ent->name, [0m[1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->name[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Special Case Context** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:3993[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m4007[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The `*%` pattern appears to be [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecial syntax for inserting entity names [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrather than expanding entity content [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlike the regular `%` syntax does at lines [0m[1;36m3988[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3989[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic Preservation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix must:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Maintain the `*%` pattern's intended behavior of inserting entity names[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Not modify the regular `%` parameter entity expansion logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3950[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3992[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve the existing buffer security checks and growth mechanisms[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Support the same XML parsing functionality without breaking existing tests[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: `parser.c`  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Line**: [0m[1;36m4005[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, [0m[1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->name[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Locate the vulnerable line** in `parser.c` at line [0m[1;36m4005[0m[39m within the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` function[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Replace the length parameter** from `ent->length` to `[0m[1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure the copy operation only reads the actual bytes present in the entity name [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No additional changes required** - the buffer destination checks and growth [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmechanisms in `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` are already correct[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact**: Single-line change that directly addresses the root cause [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout modifying surrounding logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Pattern Consistency**: Aligns with the established pattern used throughout the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:4646[0m[39m, valid.[0m[1;92mc:1027[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where entity/element names are always paired[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith `[0m[1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Semantic Correctness**: The `*%` pattern is attempting to insert the entity [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname, not expand its content. Using `[0m[1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` correctly calculates the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength of what is actually being copied[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Side Effects**: [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not modify the regular `%` entity expansion logic[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not alter buffer management functions[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not affect entity creation or storage[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not change the parser's overall behavior[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Security Preservation**: Maintains all existing security checks in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` including:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maximum buffer size limits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m763[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Buffer growth with overflow protection [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m769[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m773[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it preserves existing logic**:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `*%` special case remains functional, still parsing entity references and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madding entity names to the buffer[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All other entity expansion paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m handling, character references, regular [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`%` expansion, general entities[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain unchanged[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Buffer management and security checks continue to operate as designed[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix only corrects the length calculation to match the source buffer size[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it addresses the issue**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Eliminates the size mismatch between source buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and copy length [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m48[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents memcpy from reading beyond allocated heap boundaries[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The correct length ensures only the entity name bytes are copied[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer will no longer detect heap-buffer-overflow since the read will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstay within bounds[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects and mitigation**:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected**: The fix corrects a clear bug where the wrong field was used[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Testing consideration**: The `*%` pattern behavior may be undocumented/rarely [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused, but the fix implements what the code clearly intended [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcopying the entity [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Backward compatibility**: If the original behavior was somehow intentional [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mwhich is highly unlikely given it causes memory corruption[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the entity content [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be used instead: `[0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->content, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, the context strongly suggests the name should be inserted, not the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Consideration[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf the `*%` pattern was intended to expand entity content [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot insert the name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe fix would be:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->content, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, this is unlikely because:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The regular `%` syntax already handles content expansion [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3988[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3989[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Having two syntaxes for the same operation would be redundant[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code structure suggests name insertion was intended[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe primary fix using `[0m[1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is the correct solution based on code [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39manalysis and established patterns.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
